            function gameStart() {
                if (!window.app || !app.gameStart) {
                    setTimeout(gameStart, 250);
                    return;
                }
                app.gameStart();
            }
            function gameClose() {
                if (!app)
                    return;
                app.gameClose();
            }
            function mobvistaGameReady() {
                window.gameReady && window.gameReady();
            }
            function mobvistaGameEnd() {
                window.gameEnd && window.gameEnd();
            }
        </script>

        <script>
            var items = {};
            function applyStylePF(id, property, value) {
                if (!items[id]) {
                    items[id] = document.getElementById(id);
                }
                let item = items[id];
                if (item) {
                    item.style[property] = value;
                }
            }
            var progress = 0;
            function updateProgressPF() {
                if (!document.getElementById("preloader-pf")) {
                    clearTimeout(preloadIntervalPF);
                    return;
                }
                if (!window.app || !window.app.data || !window.app.data.preloader)
                    return;
                var params = window.app.data.preloader;
                var isEnabled = params.preloaderEnableBar;
                applyStylePF("loading-circle", "display", isEnabled ? "block" : "none");
                if (!isEnabled)
                    return;
                var fillColor = params.preloaderBarFillColor || "#008be8";
                var bgColor = params.preloaderBarBgColor || "#000000";
                applyStylePF("loading-circle-inner", "backgroundColor", fillColor);
                progress += 0.4;
                if (progress > 100) {
                    progress = 100;
                }
                var value = progress * 3.6;
                if (progress > 50) {
                    value = value - 180;
                    applyStylePF("loading-circle-inner", "backgroundImage", `linear-gradient(${value}deg, transparent 50%, ${fillColor} 50%), linear-gradient(0deg, ${bgColor} 50%, transparent 50%)`, );
                } else {
                    applyStylePF("loading-circle-inner", "backgroundImage", `linear-gradient(${value}deg, transparent 50%, ${bgColor} 50%), linear-gradient(0deg, ${bgColor} 50%, transparent 50%)`, );
                }
                var barScale = params.preloaderBarScale || 1;
                barScale = (barScale - 1) / 10;
                applyStylePF("loading-circle", "transform", `scale(${1.1 + barScale})`);
            }
            updateProgressPF();
            var preloadIntervalPF = setInterval(updateProgressPF, 30);
        </script>
